[ 1 ]
LAW DEPARTMENT
 LIST OF NOTARIES APPOINTED BY GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU AND IN PRACTICE AT 
THE BEGINNING OF THE YEAR 2024 - PUBLISHED
[G.O.Ms.No.154, Law Department, 30th January 2024.]
No. II(2)/LAW/58(C)/2024.
In exercise of the powers conferred by Section 6 of the Notaries Act, 1952 (Central Act III of 1952), 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby publishes the following list of Notaries appointed by the Government of 
Tamil Nadu and practice at the begining of the year 2024.
